## 3. Recommendations

### 3.1 🚨 Immediate Actions (Within 24 Hours)

1. **Incident Response Activation**
   - Activate security incident response team
   - Document all findings for investigation
   - Preserve evidence for analysis

### 3.2 Short-term Improvements (Within 1 Week)

1. **Credential Management**
   - Force password reset for affected accounts
   - Implement multi-factor authentication
   - Review privileged access management

2. **Monitoring Enhancement**
   - Deploy continuous dark web monitoring
   - Set up automated alerts for brand mentions
   - Increase logging and retention

### 3.3 Long-term Security Posture (Within 1 Month)

1. **Data Loss Prevention**
   - Implement DLP solutions
   - Classify and tag sensitive data
   - Regular data exposure assessments

2. **Security Awareness**
   - Conduct phishing simulations
   - Dark web awareness training
   - Update security policies

This research was conducted in accordance with:
- Authorized security testing agreement
- Applicable privacy and data protection laws
- Ethical hacking guidelines and best practices

All activities were defensive in nature and limited to:
- Identifying exposed organizational data
- Monitoring for threats against the organization
- Assessing security posture from an external perspective

No unauthorized access, data exfiltration, or malicious activities were performed.
